# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Prometheus Alertmanager Notification Pipeline

## Your Task

Trace the alertmanager notification pipeline from a firing alert to the receiver dispatch in prometheus/alertmanager. Find Go source files implementing: alert ingestion, the routing tree traversal, the inhibition check, the silence check, and the final notifier dispatch.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

Perfect! I've completed the analysis of the Prometheus Alertmanager notification pipeline and created a comprehensive answer document at `/workspace/answer.json`.

## Summary

I've traced the complete notification pipeline in the Prometheus Alertmanager codebase (github.com/sourcegraph/alertmanager), identifying the key Go source files and symbols that implement each stage:

### Key Components:

1. **Alert Ingestion** - `api/v2/api.go::postAlertsHandler`: HTTP endpoint that receives and validates incoming alerts

2. **Routing Tree Traversal** - `dispatch/dispatch.go::Dispatcher` and `dispatch/route.go::Route`: The dispatcher subscribes to incoming alerts and uses the routing tree to match each alert to relevant routes

3. **Inhibition Check** - `inhibit/inhibit.go::Inhibitor::Mutes()`: Evaluates inhibition rules to suppress notifications when certain conditions are met

4. **Silence Check** - `silence/silence.go::Silencer::Mutes()`: Queries active/pending silences to determine if alerts should be silenced

5. **Notification Pipeline** - `notify/notify.go::PipelineBuilder`: Builds a chain of stages (MuteStage for inhibition, TimeActiveStage, TimeMuteStage, MuteStage for silence) that process alerts before dispatch

6. **Final Notifier Dispatch** - `notify/notify.go::createReceiverStage()`: Creates per-receiver pipelines that handle deduplication, retry logic, and actual notification delivery to integrations

The answer document includes all relevant files, key symbols, the execution chain, and a detailed narrative explaining how each component integrates with the others.

This and\\n836: \\t// the use of post-filter functions is the trivial solution for now.\\n837: \\tvar res []*pb.Silence\\n838: \\n839: \\tif q.ids != nil {\\n840: \\t\\tfor _, id := range q.ids {\\n841: \\t\\t\\tif s, ok := s.st[id]; ok {\\n842: \\t\\t\\t\\tres = append(res, s.Silence)\\n843: \\t\\t\\t}\\n844: \\t\\t}\\n845: \\t} else {\\n846: \\t\\tfor _, sil := range s.st {\\n847: \\t\\t\\tres = append(res, sil.Silence)\\n848: \\t\\t}\\n849: \\t}\\n850: \\n851: \\tvar resf []*pb.Silence\\n852: \\tfor _, sil := range res {\\n853: \\t\\tremove := false\\n854: \\t\\tfor _, f := range q.filters {\\n855: \\t\\t\\tok, err := f(sil, s, now)\\n856: \\t\\t\\tif err != nil {\\n857: \\t\\t\\t\\treturn nil, s.version, err\\n858: \\t\\t\\t}\\n859: \\t\\t\\tif !ok {\\n860: \\t\\t\\t\\tremove = true\\n861: \\t\\t\\t\\tbreak\\n862: \\t\\t\\t}\\n863: \\t\\t}\\n864: \\t\\tif !remove {\\n865: \\t\\t\\tresf = append(resf, cloneSilence(sil))\\n866: \\t\\t}\\n867: \\t}\\n868: \\n869: \\treturn resf, s.version, nil\\n870: }\\n871: \\n872: // loadSnapshot loads a snapshot generated by Snapshot() into the state.\\n873: // Any previous state is wiped.\\n874: func (s *Silences) loadSnapshot(r io.Reader) error {\\n875: \\tst, err := decodeState(r)\\n876: \\tif err != nil {\\n877: \\t\\treturn err\\n878: \\t}\\n879: \\tfor _, e := range st {\\n880: \\t\\t// Comments list was moved to a single comment. We don't\\n941: \\t\\t\\t\\t// propagate oversized messages because they're sent to\\n942: \\t\\t\\t\\t// all nodes already.\\n943: \\t\\t\\t\\ts.broadcast(b)\\n944: \\t\\t\\t\\ts.metrics.propagatedMessagesTotal.Inc()\\n945: \\t\\t\\t\\ts.logger.Debug(\\\"Gossiping new silence\\\", \\\"silence\\\", e)\\n946: \\t\\t\\t}\\n947: \\t\\t}\\n948: \\t}\\n949: \\treturn nil\\n950: }\\n951: \\n952: // SetBroadcast sets the provided function as the one creating data to be\\n953: // broadcast.\\n954: func (s *Silences) SetBroadcast(f func([]byte)) {\\n955: \\ts.mtx.Lock()\\n956: \\ts.broadcast = f\\n957: \\ts.mtx.Unlock()\\n958: }\\n959: \\n960: type state map[string]*pb.MeshSilence\\n961: \\n962: // merge returns two bools: the first is true when merge caused a state change. The second\\n963: // is true if that state change added a new silence. In other words, the second return is\\n964: // true whenever a silence with a new ID has been added to the state as a result of merge.\\n965: func (s state) merge(e *pb.MeshSilence, now time.Time) (bool, bool) {\\n966: \\tid := e.Silence.Id\\n967: \\tif e.ExpiresAt.Before(now) {\\n968: \\t\\treturn false, false\\n969: \\t}\\n970: \\t// Comments list was moved to a single comment. Apply upgrade\\n971: \\t// on silences received from peers.\\n972: \\tif len(e.Silence.Comments) > 0 {\\n973: \\t\\te.Silence.Comment = e.Silence.Comments[0].Comment\\n974: \\t\\te.Silence.CreatedBy = e.Silence.Comments[0].Author\\n975: \\t\\te.Silence.Comments = nil\\n976: \\t}\\n977: \\n978: \\tprev, ok := s[id]\\n979: \\tif !ok || prev.Silence.UpdatedAt.Before(e.Silence.UpdatedAt) {\\n980: \\t\\ts[id] = e\\n981: \\t\\treturn true, !ok\\n982: \\t}\\n983: \\treturn false, false\\n984: }\\n985: \\n986: func (s state) MarshalBinary() ([]byte, error) {\\n987: \\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\\n988: \\n989: \\tfor _, e := range s {\\n990: \\t\\tif _, err := pbutil.WriteDelimited(&buf, e); Muter interface.\n113: func (s *Silencer) Mutes(lset model.LabelSet) bool {\n114: \tfp := lset.Fingerprint()\n115: \tactiveIDs, pendingIDs, markerVersion, _ := s.marker.Silenced(fp)\n116: \n117: \tvar (\n118: \t\terr        error\n119: \t\tallSils    []*pb.Silence\n120: \t\tnewVersion = markerVersion\n121: \t)\n122: \tif markerVersion == s.silences.Version() {\n123: \t\ttotalSilences := len(activeIDs) + len(pendingIDs)\n124: \t\t// No new silences added, just need to check which of the old\n125: \t\t// silences are still relevant and which of the pending ones\n126: \t\t// have become active.\n127: \t\tif totalSilences == 0 {\n128: \t\t\t// Super fast path: No silences ever applied to this\n129: \t\t\t// alert, none have been added. We are done.\n130: \t\t\treturn false\n131: \t\t}\n132: \t\t// This is still a quite fast path: No silences have been added,\n133: \t\t// we only need to check which of the applicable silences are\n134: \t\t// currently active. So let's do it in any case. Note that we cannot reuse the\n161: \t// current ID slices for concurrency reasons.\n162: \tactiveIDs, pendingIDs = nil, nil\n163: \tnow := s.silences.nowUTC()\n164: \tfor _, sil := range allSils \tsort.Strings(pendingIDs)\n183: \n184: \ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, activeIDs, pendingIDs)\n185: \n186: \treturn len(activeIDs) > 0\n187: }\n188: \n189: // Silences holds a silence \t\t)\n317: \t}\n318: \treturn m\n319: }\n320: \n321: // Options exposes configuration options for creating a new Silences object.\n322: // Its zero value is a safe default.\n323: type Options struct {\n324: \t// A snapshot file or reader from which the initial state is loaded.\n325: \t// None or only one of them must be set.\n326: \tSnapshotFile   string\n327: \tSnapshotReader io.Reader\n328: \n329: \t// Retention time for newly created Silences. If the snapshot\n392: // file is set, a snapshot is written to it afterwards.\n393: // Terminates on receiving from stopc.\n394: // If not nil, the last argument is an override for what to do as part of the maintenance - for advanced usage.\n395: func (s *Silences) Maintenance(interval time.Duration, snapf string, stopc <-chan struct{}, override MaintenanceFunc) {\n396: \tif interval == 0 || stopc == nil {\n397: \t\ts.logger.Error(\"interval or stop signal are missing - not running maintenance\")\n398: \t\treturn\n399: \t}\n400: \tt := s.clock.NewTicker(interval)\n401: \tdefer t.Stop()\n402: \n403: \tvar doMaintenance MaintenanceFunc\n404: \tdoMaintenance = func() (int64, error) {\n405: \t\tvar size int64\n406: \n407: \t\tif _, err := s.GC(); err != nil {\n408: \t\t\treturn size, err\n409: \t\t}\n410: \t\tif snapf == \"\" {\n411: \t\t\treturn size, nil\n412: \t\t}\n413: \t\tf, err := openReplace(snapf)\n414: \t\tif err != nil {\n415: \t\t\treturn size, err\n416: \t\t}\n417: \t\tif size, err = s.Snapshot(f); err != nil {\n418: \t\t\tf.Close()\n419: \t\t\treturn size, err\n420: \t\t}\n421: \t\treturn size, f.Close()\n422: \t}\n423: \n424: \tif override != nil {\n425: \t\tdoMaintenance = override\n426: \t}\n427: \n428: \trunMaintenance := func(do MaintenanceFunc) error {\n429: \t\ts.metrics.maintenanceTotal.Inc()\n430: \t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Running maintenance\")\n431: \t\tstart := s.nowUTC()\n432: \t\tsize, err := do()\n433: \t\ts.metrics.snapshotSize.Set(float64(size))\n434: \t\tif err != nil {\n435: \t\t\ts.metrics.maintenanceErrorsTotal.Inc()\n436: \t\t\treturn err\n437: \t\t}\n438: \t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Maintenance done\", \"duration\", s.clock.Since(start), \"size\", size)\n439: \t\treturn nil\n440: \t}\n441: \n442: Loop:\n443: \tfor {\n444: \t\tselect {\n445: \t\tcase <-stopc:\n446: \t\t\tbreak Loop\n447: \t\tcase <-t.C:\n448: \t\t\tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n449: \t\t\t\t// @tjhop: this should probably log at error level\n450: \t\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Running maintenance failed\", \"err\", err)\n451: \t\t\t}\n452: \t\t}\n453: \t}\n454: \n455: \t// No need for final maintenance if we don't want to snapshot.\n456: \tif snapf == \"\" {\n457: \t\treturn\n458: \t}\n459: \tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n460: \t\t// @tjhop: this should probably log at error level\n461: \t\ts.logger.Info(\"Creating shutdown snapshot failed\", \"err\", err)\n462: \t}\n463: }\n464: \n465: // GC runs a garbage collection that removes silences that have ended longer\n466: // than the configured retention time ago.\n467: func (s *Silences) GC() (int, error) {\n468: \tstart := time.Now()\n469: \tdefer func() { s.metrics.gcDuration.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds()) }()\n470: \n471: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n472: \tvar n int\n473: \n474: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n475: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n476: \n477: \tfor id, sil := range s.st {\n478: \t\tif sil.ExpiresAt.IsZero() {\n479: \t\t\treturn n, errors.New(\"unexpected zero expiration timestamp\")\n480: \t\t}\n481: \t\tif !sil.ExpiresAt.After(now) {\n482: \t\t\tdelete(s.st, id)\n483: \t\t\tdelete(s.mc, sil.Silence.Id)\n484: \t\t\tn++\n485: \t\t}\n486: \t}\n487: \n488: \treturn n, nil\n489: }\n490: \n491: func validateMatcher(m *pb.Matcher) error {\n492: \tif !compat.IsValidLabelName(model.LabelName(m.Name)) {\n493: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label name %q\", m.Name)\n494: \t}\n495: \tswitch m.Type {\n496: \tcase pb.Matcher_EQUAL, pb.Matcher_NOT_EQUAL:\n497: \t\tif !model.LabelValue(m.Pattern).IsValid() {\n498: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label value %q\", m.Pattern)\n499: \t\t}\n500: \tcase pb.Matcher_REGEXP, pb.Matcher_NOT_REGEXP:\n501: \t\tif _, err := regexp.Compile(m.Pattern); If a silence with the ID already exists and the modification\n594: // modifies history, the old silence gets expired and a new one is created.\n595: func (s *Silences) Set(sil *pb.Silence) error {\n596: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n597: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n598: \n599: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n600: \tif sil.StartsAt.IsZero() {\n601: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n602: \t}\n603: \n604: \tif err := err != nil {\n617: \t\t\treturn err\n618: \t\t}\n619: \t\treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n620: \t}\n621: \n622: \t// If we got here it's either a new silence or a replacing one (which would\n623: \t// also create a new silence) so we need to make sure we have capacity for\n624: \t// the new silence.\n625: \tif s.limits.MaxSilences != nil {\n626: \t\tif m := s.limits.MaxSilences(); m > 0 && len(s.st)+1 > m {\n627: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"exceeded maximum number of silences: %d (limit: %d)\", len(s.st), m)\n628: \t\t}\n629: \t}\n630: \n631: \tuid, err := uuid.NewV4()\n632: \tif err != nil {\n633: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"generate uuid: %w\", err)\n634: \t}\n635: \tsil.Id = uid.String()\n636: \n637: \tif sil.StartsAt.Before(now) {\n638: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n639: \t}\n640: \tsil.UpdatedAt = now\n641: \n642: \tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n643: \tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n644: \t\treturn err\n645: \t}\n646: \n647: \tif ok && getState(prev, s.nowUTC()) != types.SilenceStateExpired {\n648: \t\t// We cannot update the silence, expire the old one to leave a history of\n649: \t\t// the silence before modification.\n650: \t\tif err := !reflect.DeepEqual(a.Matchers, b.Matchers) {\n662: \t\treturn false\n663: \t}\n664: \t// Allowed timestamp modifications depend on the current time.\n665: \tswitch st := getState(a, now); st {\n666: returned if the silence already expired before it is GC'd.\n694: // If the silence is not found an error is returned.\n695: func (s *Silences) expire(id string) error {\n696: \tsil, ok :=
